 ) bijepi se naaraaz hokar congress main shaamil hue shatrughna sinha kii patni punam shatrughna sinha paanchave charan kii votigan main sabase dhani pratyaashee hai
 There are 184 candidates in this phase who have more than 1 crore assets
 is chunaav main sabase zyada dhani pratyaashee bhartiya janata party(bijepi) se chunaav lard rahe hai
 According to the Association for Democratic Reforms (ADR) report, 28 percent of the candidates have assets worth crores
 samaajawaadee party kii punam shatrughna sinha ke paas 193 karod kii sampatti he jo sabhi pratyaashiyon kii tulana main sabase zyada he
 Poonam Sinha is contesting from Lucknow parliamentary seat
 punam sinha ke baad duusare sabase dhani pratyaashee vijay kumaar mishra ke paas 177 karod kii sampatti he
 Vijay Kumar Mishra is contesting the Sitapur parliamentary seat from the Progressive Samajwadi Party (lohia)
 is list main bijepi pratyaashee jayant singh tisare number hai
